                   иCиhиaиoиsи... everything started then..

                                      __
                                      \/


                   Today  I'm  proud  to  present  my first
                   ascii  collection.  It's  a  result of a
                   couple of months less or more hard work.
                   I  never surpose that I'll be doing this
                   because  I'm  mainly  a swapper (neither
                   fast nor hot stuffer or even friendly...
                   just  quality  swapper  as  I'm  calling
                   this).  Also  I'm  a graphician, but I'm
                   not makeing such a beautiful things like
                   Lazur,  Kazik,  FadeOne,  Cougar...  and
                   many  more...  I'm rather interesting on
                   doing    logos,    sometimes    fonts...
                   Especially  Graffitti  is  my  favourite
                   style  (for now) so I'm concentrating on
                   this...

                                      __
                                      \/


                   Ascii...  I started makeing this because
                   it was nearly always better looking that
                   similar of my close friends...

                                      __
                                      \/


                   Whole  work  I've  done it's made rather
                   for fun not for status or something like
                   that...  I  hope  I'll continue this job
                   and  I'll  learn  something new with all
                   these days comming...

                                      __
                                      \/


                     иIиtи'иsи иaиlиlи иfиoиrи иfиuиnи!и

                                      __
                                      \/


                   By the way... Don't take comments to the
                   ascii for serious...

                                      __
                                      \/


                   Oh..  One  more  thing.. I'm looking for
                   ascii  colletions  of the greatest ascii
                   makers  on  the  scene...  Now I've only
                   about  10  mb  of this stuff from latest
                   few months...
                                      __
                                      \/


                   I'm   looking   for  an  ascii-group  to
                   join...

                                      __
                                      \/


                          иEиnиjиoиyи иtиhиeи иaиsиcиiиiи!и




                                      signed: Sharp/Anadune
